Below are the top 4 destinations in Switzerland:\n\nThe city of Lucerne \nThe city of Lucerne is situated on the shores of the picturesque Lake Lucerne, home to the world-famous Chapel Bridge. It is a paradise for skiing and mountaineering. Visitors can admire Zermatt\u2019s breathtaking views from atop Gornergrat at 3,089m when taking the cable car ride. The traditional wood houses with red rooftops make a memorable impression.\n\nInterlaken\nInterlaken is a popular resort town nestled between two jewel-toned lakes, Thun and Brienz. The fresh air, spectacular natural scenery of snow-capped mountains make it an ideal destination for outdoor activities like hiking, mountain climbing and kayaking. The old towns and tourist caf\u00e9s are also worth exploring.\n\nIn summary, with incredible natural wonders and famous tourist cities, Switzerland will surely give you an unforgettable trip. Gi\u00e0u v\u1eadt ch\u1ea5t v\u00e0 gi\u00e0u th\u00f4ng tin. T\u1ea5t nhi\u00ean, c\u00f3 nh\u1eefng anh t\u00e0i ph\u1ea5t l\u00ean nh\u1edd v\u1eadn may, kh\u00f4ng c\u1ea7n t\u1edbi ki\u1ebfn th\u1ee9c v\u00e0 c\u0169ng ch\u1eb3ng c\u1ea7n ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u1ecdc s\u00e1ch.\n\nTrong game cu\u1ed9c \u0111\u1eddi, v\u1eadn may gi\u1ed1ng nh\u01b0 m\u1ed9t vi\u00ean x\u00fac x\u1eafc tr\u00ean b\u00e0n c\u01b0\u1ee3c. \nTr\u00f4ng c\u1eady v\u00e0o v\u1eadn may ch\u1eb3ng kh\u00e1c g\u00ec n\u00e9m x\u00fac x\u1eafc xu\u1ed1ng b\u00e0n quay ru l\u00e9t, v\u00e0o \u0111\u1ecf th\u00ec l\u00ean m\u00e2y, v\u00e0o \u0111en th\u00ec xu\u1ed1ng v\u1ef1c. \nV\u1eadn may trong game \u0111\u1eddi c\u0169ng gi\u1ed1ng h\u1ea1t x\u00fac x\u1eafc tr\u00ean b\u00e0n c\u1edd.\nGi\u1ed1ng nh\u01b0 tr\u00f2 c\u1edd T\u1ef7 ph\u00fa, \u0111i k\u00e8m v\u1eadn may, \u0111\u00fang l\u00fac \u0111\u00fang th\u1eddi \u0111i\u1ec3m, bi\u1ebft ch\u01a1i bi\u1ebft ngh\u0129 d\u1ef1a tr\u00ean Tr\u00ed tu\u1ec7, v\u1ec1 l\u00e2u d\u00e0i s\u1ebd out tr\u00ecnh c\u1ea3 l\u00e0ng h\u01a1n. \nGame \u0111\u1eddi l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t chu\u1ed7i ng\u1eabu nhi\u00ean.
